# 文档总览

> **Language note** — This index is Chinese-only by design: it links into Chinese internal product / architecture / review documents. English-mirrored entry points covering developer onboarding live at:
>
> - [../README.en.md](../README.en.md) — project overview
> - [../CONTRIBUTING.en.md](../CONTRIBUTING.en.md) — contribution guide
> - [getting-started.en.md](getting-started.en.md) — developer quickstart (`npm run quickstart` / Docker-first)
>
> 中文读者请直接往下读；本索引下方所有文档默认为中文。

## 根定位（必读）

- **[positioning/HELM_FOR_DELIVERY_ENGINEERS_V1.md](positioning/HELM_FOR_DELIVERY_ENGINEERS_V1.md)** — Helm 的一页根定位：面向 AI 生态交付工程师，差异化表（vs Coze / 悟空 / Dify / LangGraph / LangChain）+ 7 个 code-backed value point + 30 分钟 onboarding 锚点 + 卖 / 不卖边界。所有下游文档（README、AGENTS、WORKING-CONTEXT、release plan）从这里派生。

## 当前主干先读

先按这个顺序理解当前仓库，而不是按旧本地 `helm/` 子目录的目录假设理解：

0. **【五月窗口推进依据】** [HELM_OPEN_SOURCE_AND_CLOUD_TRIAL_LAUNCH_PLAN_V1.md](product/HELM_OPEN_SOURCE_AND_CLOUD_TRIAL_LAUNCH_PLAN_V1.md) — 五月开源 + 云端试用四项关键决策与五周分解；配套：
   - [HELM_OPEN_SOURCE_COMMERCIAL_BOUNDARY_PLAN.md](product/HELM_OPEN_SOURCE_COMMERCIAL_BOUNDARY_PLAN.md) — Apache-2.0 open core + commercial runtime + partner delivery 商业边界：开源作为采用引擎 / 标准层 / 伙伴生态入口，商业版保留 Cloud / Enterprise / Certified workflow packs / official connectors / audit / custom / partner delivery
   - [GOVERNANCE.md](../GOVERNANCE.md) — 开源治理、maintainer scope、release gate、认证和品牌边界
   - [HELM_OPEN_CORE_COMMERCIAL_MATRIX.md](product/HELM_OPEN_CORE_COMMERCIAL_MATRIX.md) — open core / cloud / enterprise / custom / deferred 能力矩阵，避免把开源和商业版边界混写
   - [HELM_TRADEMARK_AND_BRAND_USAGE_GUIDE.md](product/HELM_TRADEMARK_AND_BRAND_USAGE_GUIDE.md) — Helm Core / Cloud / Enterprise / Official / Certified 的品牌使用边界；非法律意见
   - [HELM_CERTIFIED_ECOSYSTEM_CHECKLIST.md](product/HELM_CERTIFIED_ECOSYSTEM_CHECKLIST.md) — Certified Connector / Workflow Pack / Partner / Deployment 的第一版人工认证清单
   - [HELM_FOUNDER_LED_OPC_OPERATING_PROTOCOL.md](product/HELM_FOUNDER_LED_OPC_OPERATING_PROTOCOL.md) — startup / OPC 阶段的 founder-led 执行协议：owner 最终决策，Codex 准备 decision packet 与 5 个评审视角，Claude Code bounded implementation；真实 public trial / production data / privacy / security / public claim 仍升级到 evidence gate 或 independent review
   - [HELM_FOUNDER_OPERATING_MODE_REQUIREMENTS.md](product/HELM_FOUNDER_OPERATING_MODE_REQUIREMENTS.md) — Founder Operating Mode 产品化需求：把 founder operating loop 收成 `observe -> judge -> assign -> bounded action -> audit -> follow up -> improve Helm` 的创始人经营闭环；当前只授权 docs / planning / future implementation breakdown，不授权 schema、API、runtime、UI、自动执行或外部副作用
   - [HELM_FOUNDER_DECISION_PACKET_P0_RELEASE_AND_ADVANCEMENT.md](_planning/HELM_FOUNDER_DECISION_PACKET_P0_RELEASE_AND_ADVANCEMENT.md) — 第一份 founder-led decision packet：先修 public-release guard，再推进 Business Advancement disabled internal gate；production query adoption 继续 No-Go
   - [HELM_P0_PUBLIC_RELEASE_HYGIENE_CLOSEOUT.md](reviews/HELM_P0_PUBLIC_RELEASE_HYGIENE_CLOSEOUT.md) — P0 public-release hygiene 收口报告：`check:public-release` 当前恢复 PASS，tenant/shared-layer blocker 清零；Business Advancement production query adoption 仍 No-Go
   - [HELM_RDS_SECRET_HISTORY_REMEDIATION_PLAN.md](reviews/HELM_RDS_SECRET_HISTORY_REMEDIATION_PLAN.md) — RDS 历史凭据泄露 remediation：当前文件树已清，但 `origin/main` 历史仍需云端轮换 + 受控 history rewrite 才能解除 P0
   - [HELM_GITHUB_APACHE2_PUBLIC_RELEASE_EXECUTION_PLAN_TO_2026_05_31.md](reviews/HELM_GITHUB_APACHE2_PUBLIC_RELEASE_EXECUTION_PLAN_TO_2026_05_31.md) — 以 `2026-05-31` 为目标日的 GitHub Apache-2.0 公开发布倒排执行计划：唯一目标是 public release，关键路径固定为 secret rotation → history rewrite → real public mirror clean receipt → public docs/governance review → rehearsal → final Go/No-Go → GitHub release；6 月商业化试点准备动作明确降级到后续目标
   - [HELM_SECRET_ROTATION_AND_RELEASE_UNBLOCK_CHECKLIST_2026_05_20.md](operations/HELM_SECRET_ROTATION_AND_RELEASE_UNBLOCK_CHECKLIST_2026_05_20.md) — 面向 `2026-05-20` 的 secret rotation / revocation 单日执行清单：定义完成口径、Go/No-Go 条件、non-secret receipt 要求与日终汇报格式，用于把 public release 的唯一 P0 blocker 从“知道要做”推进到“已处理并可留档”
   - [HELM_PUBLIC_RELEASE_REWRITE_REF_INVENTORY_2026_05_22.md](internal/HELM_PUBLIC_RELEASE_REWRITE_REF_INVENTORY_2026_05_22.md) — 面向 history rewrite maintenance window 的 remote ref 快照：汇总 `origin` 远端 refs 范围、直接相关 refs 和当前 prep-only 判断，用于 rewrite 前的协作者恢复范围确认
   - [HELM_PUBLIC_RELEASE_FREEZE_AND_HISTORY_REWRITE_NOTICE_TEMPLATE_2026_05.md](internal/HELM_PUBLIC_RELEASE_FREEZE_AND_HISTORY_REWRITE_NOTICE_TEMPLATE_2026_05.md) — 协作者 freeze / history rewrite / recovery 通知模板：包含短版、完整版、freeze start 和 rewrite complete 恢复话术
   - [HELM_PUBLIC_GITHUB_SURFACE_REVIEW_2026_05_26.md](reviews/HELM_PUBLIC_GITHUB_SURFACE_REVIEW_2026_05_26.md) — `2026-05-26` public GitHub surface 人工审校结果：记录 README / GOVERNANCE / CONTRIBUTING / public roadmap / public trial runbook / launch draft 的 repo-side 审校范围、已修复的 placeholder / dead-link 问题，以及 release 仍保持 No-Go 的原因
   - [HELM_BUSINESS_ADVANCEMENT_FOUNDER_INTERNAL_GATE_CLOSEOUT.md](reviews/HELM_BUSINESS_ADVANCEMENT_FOUNDER_INTERNAL_GATE_CLOSEOUT.md) — Founder-led Business Advancement internal gate：只允许 disabled internal dogfooding preparation；production query / runtime integration / public trial 继续 No-Go
   - [HELM_BUSINESS_ADVANCEMENT_INTERNAL_DOGFOOD_PACKET_CLOSEOUT.md](reviews/HELM_BUSINESS_ADVANCEMENT_INTERNAL_DOGFOOD_PACKET_CLOSEOUT.md) — Business Advancement disabled internal dogfooding packet：用 injected-row prototype 输出生成 review-only candidate groups 与 stop conditions，不接 production query
   - [HELM_BUSINESS_ADVANCEMENT_PHASE3V_LOCAL_CALIBRATION_REHEARSAL_CLOSEOUT.md](reviews/HELM_BUSINESS_ADVANCEMENT_PHASE3V_LOCAL_CALIBRATION_REHEARSAL_CLOSEOUT.md) — Phase 3V local calibration rehearsal：远端 DB 不可达时用本地隔离库验证 Phase 3P→3Q→3R→3S 工具链仍可跑，且仍保持 production/runtime No-Go
   - [HELM_BUSINESS_ADVANCEMENT_PHASE3_RUNTIME_ENABLEMENT_REVIEW_V1.md](reviews/HELM_BUSINESS_ADVANCEMENT_PHASE3_RUNTIME_ENABLEMENT_REVIEW_V1.md) — Phase 3 受限解禁范围、6 项硬前置、回滚剧本
   - [HELM_PHASE3_REQUIRED_REVIEWER_CANDIDATE_FRAMEWORK_V1.md](reviews/HELM_PHASE3_REQUIRED_REVIEWER_CANDIDATE_FRAMEWORK_V1.md) — 5 角色 Required Reviewer 候选名单框架（必备 / 优先 / 否决 / 时间承诺 / 互斥规则 / 3 次会议节奏）
   - [HELM_PUBLIC_TRIAL_DATA_POLICY_V1.md](legal/HELM_PUBLIC_TRIAL_DATA_POLICY_V1.md) — 30/7 数据保留期、no-SLA 立场、用户权利
   - [HELM_PACK_A_PILOT_AGREEMENT_TEMPLATE_V1.md](legal/HELM_PACK_A_PILOT_AGREEMENT_TEMPLATE_V1.md) — Pack A 4 周 paid pilot 协议起草模板；非法律意见，需客户/Helm 法务终审
   - [HELM_PACK_A_DPA_TEMPLATE_V1.md](legal/HELM_PACK_A_DPA_TEMPLATE_V1.md) — Pack A 数据处理协议模板；限定 pilot 目的、90 天保留、子处理方、跨境说明和删除证明
   - [HELM_PRIVATE_TENANT_SEPARATION_PLAN_V1.md](internal/HELM_PRIVATE_TENANT_SEPARATION_PLAN_V1.md) — `extensions/guangpu/` 双仓库剥离执行计划
   - [HELM_PUBLIC_ROADMAP.md](roadmap/HELM_PUBLIC_ROADMAP.md) — 对外路线图（Now / Next 30 days / Later / Out of scope）
   - [PUBLIC_TRIAL_RUNBOOK.md](pilot/PUBLIC_TRIAL_RUNBOOK.md) — 公开试用用户须知 / 数据隔离 / 反馈渠道 / oncall 操作 / 状态机
   - [HELM_RETENTION_STATUS_CARD_DESIGN_V1.md](product/HELM_RETENTION_STATUS_CARD_DESIGN_V1.md) — `/settings/billing` 数据保留状态卡片设计与组件契约

## 当前主干 reality

- 当前执行入口仍然是根目录 `app/`
- `data/queries.ts` 仍然是当前主干真实存在的兼容查询面
- 邮件连接器主线当前已切到阿里邮箱（IMAP 同步 + 系统 SMTP 发信 + 手动显式发送），底层仍保留 `GMAIL` 枚举兼容映射
- 当前主干没有可执行目录叫 `apps/helm-app`
- 当前主干没有可执行目录叫 `packages/helm-control`
- route/query ownership 必须先收紧，再考虑 shell thinning
- `layout / loading / error / not-found` 的收薄属于晚期动作，不是立即动作

### audits/

- [HELM_DESIGN_PRINCIPLE_AUDIT_2026-05-03.md](audits/HELM_DESIGN_PRINCIPLE_AUDIT_2026-05-03.md)
  - 以 AGENTS.md / DESIGN.md / WORKING-CONTEXT.md 为准绳，对 priority hardening 分支关键路径做的设计原则与边界审计；报告本身不声明 runtime/API/UI/write 新能力成立

### root/

- [DESIGN.md](../DESIGN.md)
  - 当前固定视觉方向、页面层级、组件约束与明确禁止事项
- [WORKING-CONTEXT.md](../WORKING-CONTEXT.md)
  - 当前 active queue、短周期约束、repo-local Codex 使用姿态与执行提醒
- [GOVERNANCE.md](../GOVERNANCE.md)
  - 开源治理、maintainer scope、贡献权利、release gate、认证和品牌边界；不创建企业 SLA、商标许可或认证平台
- [.codex/config.toml](../.codex/config.toml)
  - repo-local Codex profiles、`codex_hooks` feature 与 scoped agent roles；只服务仓库执行，不扩成平台层
- [.codex/hooks.json](../.codex/hooks.json)
  - repo-local guardrails 路由；当前先覆盖 `no-verify`、`git push` 目标/dirty/upstream 提醒、配置保护、设计质量检查、`console.log/console.error/debugger/TODO: remove before merge` 检查、窄 `SessionStart` bootstrap、Stop 阶段 validation 提醒
- `scripts/codex-hooks/`
  - repo-local guardrail scripts；只做最小提醒与阻断，不扩成平台层
- `extensions/`
  - 租户客户定制需求的当前主目录；默认按 `extensions/<tenant-key>/<extension-slug>/` 落代码、文档、测试和资产，不再直接写进 shared top-level namespace
- [extensions/guangpu/README.md](../extensions/guangpu/README.md)
  - Guangpu tenant root 当前总览、tenant manifest 入口，以及 seat-profile / bi-report 两条扩展主线的协作入口
- [report-skills/README.md](../report-skills/README.md)
  - `BI report proactive push` 的 skill pack 目录约定：固定 `query.sql / schema.json / metrics.json / result-criteria.json / prompt.md / message-template.md`，当前只是 repo asset，不是 skill marketplace
- [extensions/guangpu/GUANGPU_EXTENSION_UPDATE_ISSUES_V1.md](../extensions/guangpu/GUANGPU_EXTENSION_UPDATE_ISSUES_V1.md)
  - `guangpu` 当前 extension 收口问题清单，供开发团队继续对齐 manifest、目录职责、loader 和 script truth
- [GUANGPU_ORGANIZATION_ROLE_GOAL_IMPLEMENTATION_REQUIREMENTS.md](../extensions/guangpu/docs/GUANGPU_ORGANIZATION_ROLE_GOAL_IMPLEMENTATION_REQUIREMENTS.md)
  - Guangpu tenant-private 组织 / 岗位 / 目标 / 责任路由实施需求：固定公司唯一入口、组织单元、岗位职责、目标口径、米盾映射、信号路由、坐席画像新鲜度和人工复核证据的最小 slice；继续禁止 HR 绩效、自动派工、自动通知和米盾写回
- [HELM_GUANGPU_SEAT_PROFILE_EXTENSION_KEY_BACKFILL_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_GUANGPU_SEAT_PROFILE_EXTENSION_KEY_BACKFILL_REPORT_V1.md)

### product/

- [product-principles.md](product/product-principles.md)

- [HELM_FIRST_LOOP_PRD_V1.md](product/HELM_FIRST_LOOP_PRD_V1.md)
  - planning-only 产品文档：收口 Helm 当前阶段的 onboarding / first-run / first-value 问题，定义 `setup -> signal -> suggestion -> review -> follow-through -> memory write-back -> next visit anchor` 的 horizontal first loop；planned objects 不等于 current-main schema
- [HELM_COGNITIVE_OBJECT_AND_FOUR_PLANE_CONTRACT_BASELINE_V1.md](product/HELM_COGNITIVE_OBJECT_AND_FOUR_PLANE_CONTRACT_BASELINE_V1.md)
  - 冻结 Helm 当前阶段的四层控制面和四类认知对象 contract，明确 `Belief / Goal / Committed Intention / OperatingGap` 当前映射、已成立 truth 和仍需下一层的部分
- [HELM_NARROW_TRUTH_RECONCILIATION_ENGINE_BASELINE_V1.md](product/HELM_NARROW_TRUTH_RECONCILIATION_ENGINE_BASELINE_V1.md)
  - 冻结 PR101：只在 `meeting / email / CRM / report` 四类输入之间建立一条窄的 truth reconciliation engine，固定 `resolved / unresolved / confidence / evidence chain / operator review required` 输出，不做 schema migration 或 ontology platform
- [HELM_OPERATING_GAP_OBJECT_BASELINE_V1.md](product/HELM_OPERATING_GAP_OBJECT_BASELINE_V1.md)
  - 冻结 PR102：把 `TruthConflict / ProblemSpace / CompositionFailure` 收成 `operator-governance projection` 的 `OperatingGap` object，并接到 runtime operator surface；当前仍不是 canonical persisted object
- [HELM_BUSINESS_LOOP_OPERATING_GAP_WIRING_BASELINE_V1.md](product/HELM_BUSINESS_LOOP_OPERATING_GAP_WIRING_BASELINE_V1.md)
  - 冻结 PR103：把 `missing-kpi-link` 作为 business-loop `OperatingGap` 接到 `/operating` 首屏，前置 KPI 链缺口；当前仍不做 canonical KPI object 或 dashboard 扩面
- [HELM_BUSINESS_LOOP_GAP_AGGREGATION_BASELINE_V1.md](product/HELM_BUSINESS_LOOP_GAP_AGGREGATION_BASELINE_V1.md)
  - 冻结 PR104：把 business-loop gap 收成共享 `businessLoopGapSummary` runtime contract，让 `/operating` 和 runtime operator panel 复用同一份 summary；当前仍不做 schema migration 或 dashboard 扩面
- [HELM_BUSINESS_LOOP_GAP_READOUT_BASELINE_V1.md](product/HELM_BUSINESS_LOOP_GAP_READOUT_BASELINE_V1.md)
  - 冻结 PR105：把共享 `businessLoopGapSummary` 接到 `dashboard` 与 `reports` 的 operator-governance readout，让这些页面前置同一份主业务闭环缺口；当前仍不做 schema migration、KPI canonicalization 或 dashboard analytics 改造

  - **【Phase 3U Live Calibration Unblock Preflight】** script-only、no-DB-access 纯函数前置检查工具，在 Phase 3T DB 不可达记录之后固化重跑 Phase 3P → 3Q → 3R → 3S 所需的精确条件与安全命令链；仅读取 argv/env，不访问 DB/文件系统/网络/Prisma；校验七项条件（`DATABASE_URL` 存在且协议为 mysql、DB host 非本地地址、真实非 dummy workspaceId、有效 referenceClockIso、take 整数 1..500），全部通过时 `liveCalibrationReady=true`（exit 0）并输出精确 4 条 safeCommandChain（3P collector → 3Q intake → 3R preflight → 3S packet），否则 exit 2；`localhost`/`127.0.0.1`/`::1` 仅允许开发验证，不能解锁 live calibration；dummy workspaceId `db-reachability-probe-only` 明确拒绝；`redactedDatabaseTarget` 仅含 protocol/host/database，不含完整 URL/用户名/密码；`resolvedWorkspaceIdPresence` 为布尔值，不暴露实际 workspaceId；`productionAdoptionAllowed`/`runtimeIntegrationAllowed`/`dbAccessAttempted`/`filesWritten` 始终 false；liveCalibrationReady=true 不授权 runtime adoption，下一步仍须完整执行 safeCommandChain 并召开人工评审会议起草独立实施计划

- [HELM_AGENT_RUNTIME_SUBSTRATE_PLAN_V1.md](product/HELM_AGENT_RUNTIME_SUBSTRATE_PLAN_V1.md)
  - 记录 Helm agent runtime substrate 五条基础工程线：`Run Thread`、`Operator Debugger`、`Typed Interrupt + Handoff Contract`、`Project Skill Library + Environment Contract`、`Benchmark Matrix`；当前第一层实现已经全部落地，并且下一层的前二十一刀 `run-thread result acknowledgement + environment execution seam`、`debugger request acknowledgement flow`、`run-thread request posture summary`、`active takeover seam`、`run-thread write lifecycle result flow`、`operator debugger active-control contract`、`environment execution authority`、`benchmark execution / acknowledgement workflow`、`benchmark workflow control-plane follow-through`、`run-thread write lifecycle forward flow`、`operator-active control follow-through closeout`、`thread-level closeout flow summary`、`thread-level lifecycle settlement flow`、`thread-level settlement review seam`、`thread-level closeout confirmation seam`、`thread-level closeout refresh seam`、`thread-level closeout summary seam`、`thread-level closeout resolution seam`、`thread-level closeout resolution follow-through seam`、`thread-level closeout outcome seam` 与 `thread-level close request seam` 也已接上：`trace / checkpoint resume / continuity queue / meeting runtime surface` 已共享统一 `runThread`，并补出只读 `history / variable snapshot / replay assistance / human input checkpoint / operator takeover assistance / interrupt reason / resume ask / handoff payload skeleton` debugger read model；`continuity remediation`、`checkpoint resume`、`handoff.packet.created`、`operator.takeover.requested`、`operator.takeover.acknowledged`、`operator.takeover.started`、`operator.takeover.released`、`operator.takeover.followthrough.requested`、`operator.takeover.followthrough.resolved`、`human-input.checkpoint.requested` 和 `human-input.checkpoint.acknowledged` 会回写 typed posture / contract / request ledger，`runThread.lifecycleLog` 继续把现有 write lifecycle note 收成同一份 typed ledger，而当前 takeover / human input request 的 `requested -> acknowledged` posture 也会被统一收成 `runThread.requestPosture` 并投影回 surfaces；在此之上，bounded operator control 现在还能通过 `takeover_active / takeover_released` 继续进入同一份 lifecycle ledger 和 debugger/operator surface，并显式给出 `currentOwner / latestEventKind / releasedAt / releasedBy / releaseReason`；release 之后新的 `takeoverFollowThrough` 还会继续把 active-control closeout 显式收成 `requestable / open / resolved`，并让 `runThread.forwardFlow` 在 closeout 打开时进入 `lifecycle_closeout`；现在 operator closeout 和 downstream result follow-through 还会再统一收成 canonical `runThread.closeoutFlow`，并继续收成 `runThread.settlementFlow`，显式给出 `active / closeout_open / review_open / ready_to_close / closed` 的 thread-level settlement truth、driver、owner、checkpointKey 与 nextAction，并继续投影回 meeting runtime surface、`/operating` 与 debugger snapshot；新的 `runThread.settlementReview` 则继续把 `run-thread.settlement.review.requested / resolved` 收成 explicit operator review seam，而新的 `runThread.closeoutConfirmation` 则继续把 `run-thread.closeout.confirmed` 收成 `confirmable / confirmed / stale` 的 persisted control-plane closeout truth，新的 `runThread.closeoutRefresh` 则继续把 `run-thread.closeout.refresh.requested` 收成 `requestable / open / resolved` 的 stale-closeout reopen follow-through，新的 `runThread.closeoutSummary` 则继续把 `closeoutFlow / settlementReview / closeoutConfirmation / closeoutRefresh` 统一收成 `active / review_requestable / review_open / confirmable / confirmed / refresh_requestable / refresh_open / closed` 的 canonical closeout posture，而新的 `runThread.closeoutResolution` 则继续把 `run-thread.closeout.resolution.recorded` 收成 `not_available / decision_required / close_recorded / keep_open_recorded / stale` 的 explicit close-versus-keep-open truth，新的 `runThread.closeoutResolutionFollowThrough` 则继续把 `run-thread.closeout.resolution.followthrough.requested / resolved` 收成 `not_available / requestable / open / resolved / stale` 的 post-resolution follow-through seam，新的 `runThread.closeoutOutcome` 则继续把 `closeoutResolution / closeoutResolutionFollowThrough / lifecycle(closedAt)` 统一收成 `not_available / decision_required / followthrough_required / followthrough_open / close_pending / kept_open / closed / mismatch / stale` 的 thread-level final outcome truth，而新的 `runThread.closeRequest` 则继续把 `run-thread.close.requested` 收成 `not_available / requestable / open / resolved / stale / mismatch` 的 explicit bounded runtime close seam；`human execution / guarded official write / limited auto / official follow-through` 的最新结果现在除了会被统一写成 `resultAcknowledgement` 外，还会被统一收成 thread 级 `resultFlow`，按来源给出 latest posture、attention/resolved 计数与 source-level latest result，并继续投影回 surfaces；`worker / skill / resource` 也已收成 project-scoped skill library 并继续叠加 environment contract runtime posture，把 `connector / browser / control-plane / workspace-context / official-action` seam 显式接到 meeting runtime surface 与 `/operating`，同时 `environmentContract.executionSeam` 会显式给出最新 guarded write / limited auto / official follow-through posture，新的 `environmentContract.executionAuthority` 会进一步把这些 source 的 authority truth 收成 `manual_only / review_gated / narrow_limited_auto / boundary_only`；benchmark matrix 则已把 `runtime eval / adapter conformance / boundary regression / operator usability` 四层 gate 收成统一 read model 与脚本入口，并把最新 benchmark outcome 作为 workspace-scoped runtime evidence 持久化回 surfaces；现在它还额外补上了 `benchmark.matrix.run.requested / recorded / acknowledged / followthrough.requested / followthrough.resolved` 的 typed workflow，把 `workflow.request / latestRun / acknowledgement / followThrough` 一起投影回 surfaces，其中 `official action` 仍保持 review-gated
  - `run-thread persisted control-plane lifecycle` 的第一层也已经开始接入：`RuntimeSession.controlPlaneLifecycleJson / controlPlaneLifecycleUpdatedAt` 会保存 bounded thread-level control-plane snapshot，而 `runThread.persistedControlPlaneLifecycle` 会显式告诉 operator 当前是 `missing / synced / drifted / invalid`；这一层还补上了 `compactionPolicy / reconciliationPolicy / repairPolicy / guardPolicy`，把单槽 persisted snapshot 的策略固定为 `replace_on_material_state_change`，把 reconciliation 语义固定为 `bounded_snapshot_with_event_truth_fallback`，并把 repair 边界收成 `review_first_single_slot_rewrite_only`；新的 `guardPolicy` 现在会显式给出 `fallback_to_event_truth / backfill_required / rewrite_required / reuse_current_snapshot / reuse_compacted_snapshot`，而 runtime persist helper 也已经按这同一份 policy 决定 reuse 或 rewrite；persisted snapshot 现在也会把 `resumeState / latestCheckpoint / checkpointLineageDepth / replayRequest / replayEventLogEntries / humanInputCheckpoint` 收成 material state，并额外记录 `lastRefreshReason / lastRefreshSource / writeAnchor / writeCheckpointKey / writeResumeToken`，让 replay/recovery 写路径的 bounded refresh 与 persisted snapshot 共用同一份 write-side contract；persisted lifecycle 与 operator debugger 的 `trace / replay / checkpoint` contract 也已经进入第一层，通过 `debugger.persistedLifecycleTrace` 显式给出 `backfill_required / fallback_to_event_truth / refresh_required / aligned`、当前 anchor(`checkpoint / replay / human_input`)和最新 persisted write-side state；下一阶段的第一刀现在还会继续把 `replayAssistance / persistedLifecycleTrace / checkpointLineage / humanInputCheckpoint / humanInputRequest` 收成统一 `debugger.traceContract`，显式给出 `state / driver / anchor / checkpointKey / checkpointLineageDepth / replayFidelity / humanInputRequestState / nextAction`，让 meeting runtime surface 与 `/operating` 优先消费同一份中心 debugger truth；第二刀已经把 persisted write-side anchor / refresh reason / checkpointKey / resumeToken 收成统一 `debugger.writeContract`，显式区分 `resume / replay / human_input / checkpoint` 的 bounded recovery write anchor，避免把 resume 继续混进同一条 trace 视图；第三刀现在又把 `traceContract / writeContract / takeover request-activation-followthrough / recovery failure state / remediation trace` 收成统一 `debugger.recoveryActionContract`，显式告诉 operator 当前 recovery action lifecycle 到了 `backfill_required / refresh_required / requestable / requested / acknowledged / active / followthrough_open / followthrough_resolved / applied / observe` 的哪一层；第四刀则继续把 `traceContract / writeContract / recoveryActionContract` 压成统一 `debugger.recoveryLifecycleContract`，显式告诉 operator 当前 bounded replay/recovery lifecycle 处在 `backfill_required / refresh_required / blocked / review_required / request_lane / activation_lane / followthrough_lane / applied / observe` 的哪一层；第五刀现在继续把 `traceContract / writeContract / recoveryActionContract / recoveryLifecycleContract` 压成统一 `debugger.recoveryTransitionContract`，显式告诉 operator 当前 bounded replay/recovery transition posture 处在 `backfill_required / refresh_required / blocked / review_required / transition_ready / transition_pending / transition_active / transition_resolved / observe` 的哪一层；第六刀则继续把 `traceContract / writeContract / recoveryActionContract / recoveryLifecycleContract / recoveryTransitionContract` 接成统一 `debugger.recoveryStateMachineContract`，显式给出当前 phase、currentTransition、transitionState、allowedTransitions 和 completedTransitions，让 operator 不必再从多份 contract 手工推导 bounded replay/recovery state machine；第七刀现在继续把这六层 contract 收成统一 `debugger.recoveryExecutionContract`，显式告诉 operator 当前 bounded replay/recovery execution posture 是 `backfill_required / refresh_required / review_required / blocked / executable / pending / active / applied / observe` 的哪一层，以及这一步是否已经具备 execute 条件；当前这一步则继续把同一份 execution truth 收成共享 `recoveryExecutionGuardContract`，让 `request_human_input / acknowledge_human_input / request / acknowledge / start / release / request_followthrough / resolve_followthrough` 八类 bounded write-side 校验直接消费 `allowed / reused / blocked` guard，而不是继续散落在各个 server action 和 runtime write path 里；这仍然不是完整的 persisted control plane，也不是 workflow engine
- [HELM_RUN_THREAD_PERSISTED_CONTROL_PLANE_LIFECYCLE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_RUN_THREAD_PERSISTED_CONTROL_PLANE_LIFECYCLE_REPORT_V1.md)
- [HELM_RUN_THREAD_PERSISTED_CONTROL_PLANE_LIFECYCLE_FREEZE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_RUN_THREAD_PERSISTED_CONTROL_PLANE_LIFECYCLE_FREEZE_REPORT_V1.md)
- [HELM_AGENT_RUNTIME_SUBSTRATE_PHASE1_FREEZE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_AGENT_RUNTIME_SUBSTRATE_PHASE1_FREEZE_REPORT_V1.md)
  - 当前这一阶段的总冻结报告：诚实回答 runtime substrate 五条基础线与 operator summary 链哪些已经完整成立、哪些仍需下一层、哪些边界必须继续保留；当前总结论仍然是 `已成形但仍需下一层`
  - 新的 `runThread.closeLifecycle` 进一步把 `closeoutSummary / closeoutResolution / closeoutResolutionFollowThrough / closeoutOutcome / closeRequest` 统一收成 canonical thread-level close lifecycle posture，并继续投影回 trace、meeting runtime surface、`/operating` 与 debugger snapshot；它仍然是 manual、review-first 的 close truth，不是 auto-close plane，也不是 broader execution authority
  - 新的 `runThread.closeControl` 还会继续把 `closeLifecycle / settlementFlow / closeoutSummary` 统一收成 canonical thread-level close control summary，并显式给出 `state / driver / decision / checkpointKey / currentOwner / latestUpdatedAt / nextAction`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是 broader close authority
  - 新的 `runThread.closeControlFlow` 还会继续把 `closeControl / settlementFlow / forwardFlow` 统一收成 canonical thread-level close control forward summary，并显式给出 `forwardState / settlementState / forwardAttentionCount / openCloseoutCount`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `runThread.closeDecisionFlow` 会把 `closeControlFlow / closeoutOutcome / closeRequest` 统一收成 canonical thread-level close-decision summary，并显式给出 `controlState / outcomeState / closeRequestState`
  - 新的 `runThread.closeDecisionControlSummary` 则继续把 `closeDecisionFlow / closeLifecycle / forwardFlow` 收成 operator 直接消费的 close-decision-control summary，并显式给出 `decisionState / controlState / lifecycleState / forwardState / settlementState`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `runThread.closeResolutionSummary` 会再把 `closeDecisionControlSummary / closeLifecycle / closeRequest` 压成更直接的 close-resolution posture，并显式给出 `decisionControlState / lifecycleState / closeRequestState`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `runThread.closeResolutionForwardSummary` 会再把 `closeResolutionSummary / closeDecisionControlSummary / settlementFlow / forwardFlow` 压成更直接的 close-progress posture，并显式给出 `resolutionState / decisionControlState / settlementState / forwardState / forwardAttentionCount / openCloseoutCount`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority

- [HELM_V2_1_SWARM_008_CLOSE_SETTLEMENT_ADJACENCY_PLAN_V1.md](reviews/HELM_V2_1_SWARM_008_CLOSE_SETTLEMENT_ADJACENCY_PLAN_V1.md)
  - `SWARM-008` 的历史 narrow-slice plan：`shared close / settlement adjacency surfaces` 已按 read-only parity 并入主干，plan 继续作为边界记录
  - 新的 `runThread.closeResolutionControlSummary` 会把 `closeResolutionForwardSummary / closeResolutionSummary / closeLifecycle / closeRequest` 再压成最直接的 bounded close-control posture，并显式给出 `resolutionState / forwardState / lifecycleState / closeRequestState`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `runThread.closePostureSummary` 会把 `closeResolutionControlSummary / closeResolutionForwardSummary / closeLifecycle / closeRequest` 再压成更粗粒度的 operator close verdict，直接给出 `open / close_ready / close_pending / kept_open / closed / stale / mismatch`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `runThread.closePostureForwardSummary` 会把 `closePostureSummary / closeResolutionForwardSummary / settlementFlow / forwardFlow` 再压成更直接的 operator close progress 读口，显式给出 `review_requestable / review_open / closeout_open / forward_open / close_ready / close_pending / kept_open / closed`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorControlSummary` 会把 `environmentContract.executionAuthority / executionSeam` 和 `benchmarkMatrix.workflow` 再压成跨域的 operator-facing control posture，直接给出 `boundary_only / review_gated / execution_pending / execution_review / execution_follow_through / benchmark_requested / benchmark_review / benchmark_follow_through`，并补上 `focusTitle / focusHref` 让 control summary 可以直达相关 benchmark/request sourcePage，或在 environment execution 没有可信来源页时回退到 `/operating`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorProgressSummary` 会把 `requestPosture / takeoverActivation / operatorControlSummary / closePostureForwardSummary` 再压成更直接的 Operator progress summary，显式给出 `takeover_active / takeover_requested / human_input_requested / operator_control_attention / close_attention / review_gated / steady_state`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorActionSummary` 会把 `requestPosture / takeoverActivation / operatorControlSummary / closePostureForwardSummary / operatorProgressSummary / operatorReviewActionSummary` 再压成更直接的 bounded operator next-action 读口，显式给出 `acknowledge_takeover_request / capture_human_input / complete_takeover / acknowledge_execution / review_execution / resolve_execution_followthrough / run_benchmark / acknowledge_benchmark / resolve_benchmark_followthrough / advance_close / resolve_verification / review_promotion / review_reflection_candidate / watch_reflection_job / watch_consolidation_job / keep_review_gated / observe`，并补上 `focusTitle / focusHref` 让 action summary 可直达对应对象；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorWorkSummary` 会继续把 `operatorActionSummary / operatorControlSummary / operatorReviewActionSummary / continuityQueue / critical operating gaps` 压成 workspace-level next-work 读口，直接给出 `operating_gap_attention / continuity_attention / execution_attention / benchmark_attention / review_attention / review_gated / steady_state`，并让 reflection / consolidation review 也进入同一份 workspace-level next work；当 workspace next-work 由 execution/benchmark control 驱动时，它现在也会继承 `operatorControlSummary.focusTitle / focusHref`，避免顶层 next-work 卡片丢失落点；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorCueSummary` 会继续把 `operatorWorkSummary / operatorControlSummary / operatorReviewSummary / operatorReviewActionSummary` 再压成 workspace-level top cue，直接给出 `operating_gap_attention / continuity_attention / control_attention / review_attention / review_gated / steady_state`，让 `/operating` 顶层先回答“现在 operator 最应该先看哪一类 cue，以及点去哪”；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorNextMoveSummary` 会继续把 `operatorCueSummary / operatorWorkSummary / operatorActionSummary / operatorReviewActionSummary` 再压成 workspace-level bounded next move，直接给出 `resolve_operating_gap / advance_continuity / acknowledge_execution / review_execution / resolve_execution_followthrough / run_benchmark / acknowledge_benchmark / resolve_benchmark_followthrough / resolve_verification / review_promotion / review_reflection_candidate / watch_reflection_job / watch_consolidation_job / keep_review_gated / observe`，让 `/operating` 顶层不只是知道“先看哪类 cue”，还知道“先做哪一步”；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorActionCueSummary` 会继续把 `operatorCueSummary / operatorNextMoveSummary / operatorControlSummary / operatorReviewActionSummary` 压成 workspace-level coarse action lane，只保留 `resolve_operating_gap / advance_continuity / resolve_operator_control / resolve_workspace_review / keep_review_gated / observe` 六类 bounded move，让 `/operating` 顶层先回答“该做哪类动作”，再决定是否继续下钻；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorReviewControlCueSummary` 会继续把 `operatorCueSummary / operatorActionCueSummary / operatorControlSummary / operatorReviewSummary / operatorReviewActionSummary` 压成 workspace-level secondary priority cue，只回答“下一层优先入口是 review 还是 control”，并保持 `control_priority / review_priority / review_gated / observe` 四类 posture；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorStartPointSummary` 会继续把 `operatorActionCueSummary / operatorReviewControlCueSummary` 压成 workspace-level start point，直接给出一条 primary bounded move 和一条 secondary fallback，让 `/operating` 顶层先回答“先做什么，如果这步不是 blocker，下一步去哪”；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorReviewSummary` 会把 `verificationQueue / promotionQueue / reflectionCandidates / reflectionJobs / consolidationJobs` 压成 workspace-level review posture，直接给出 `verification_attention / promotion_attention / reflection_candidate_attention / reflection_job_attention / consolidation_job_attention / clear`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority
  - 新的 `operatorReviewActionSummary` 会继续把 `operatorReviewSummary` 压成 workspace-level bounded next action，直接给出 `resolve_verification / review_promotion / review_reflection_candidate / watch_reflection_job / watch_consolidation_job / hold_review_gated`；它继续保持 manual、review-first，不是新的 authority

- [HELM_COMPANY_MEMORY_FOUR_ARM_ECONOMICS_BASELINE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_COMPANY_MEMORY_FOUR_ARM_ECONOMICS_BASELINE_REPORT_V1.md)
  - CM-EVAL-3 four-arm / economics baseline 完成报告：新增 redacted payload allowlist、`--mode=four-arm` 与 `--mode=economics`，对 no-memory / raw-context / current retrieval pack / disabled distilled-memory 四臂做 deterministic token、evidence、boundary 与 cost-per-useful-judgement proxy 检查；当前仍不证明真实 LLM 输出、生产 token bill 或用户采纳

  - [HELM_MEMORY_RETRIEVAL_PACK_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_RETRIEVAL_PACK_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-PACK-004 完成报告：新增 pure `buildMemoryRetrievalPack`，按 trust / importance / recency / promotion posture 输出 selected / omitted / fallback trace，并保留 non-commitment boundary
  - [HELM_MEMORY_RETRIEVAL_PACK_SURFACE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_RETRIEVAL_PACK_SURFACE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-PACK-004B 完成报告：把 retrieval pack trace 接入 briefing、recommendation evidence 与 meeting detail 只读 surface，同时保留 ranking owner 与 commitment 边界
  - [HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_DEDUPE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_DEDUPE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-WRITE-005 完成报告：为 meeting `MemoryFact` 写入补第一层 normalized duplicate guard、conflict candidate posture、audit metadata summary 与 source/object/fact 索引；自动 retry executor 与事务化 bulk upsert 仍待下一层
  - [HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_BATCH_FAILURE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_BATCH_FAILURE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-WRITE-005B 完成报告：为 meeting `MemoryFact` 写入补 batch write result、retryable / non-retryable / operator-review-required failure classification，以及 failure audit blocking posture；自动 retry executor 仍待下一层
  - [HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_FAILURE_REVIEW_SURFACE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_FAILURE_REVIEW_SURFACE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-WRITE-005C 完成报告：把 `MEETING_MEMORY_FACT_WRITE_FAILED` audit payload 接到 diagnostics 只读 failure review readout，展示 blocked / partial-failed batch、retryable / operator-review-required count 与 failure reason；后续 read-only operator queue substrate 见 MEM-WRITE-005D，自动 retry executor 仍待下一层
  - [HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_OPERATOR_QUEUE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_OPERATOR_QUEUE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-WRITE-005D 完成报告：把 failure audit sample 转成只读 operator queue substrate，展示人工确认重试、冲突复核、源数据修复、payload 检查、payload status 与截断信息；自动 retry executor 与 owner-aware operator workflow 仍待下一层
  - [HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_RETRY_CONTRACT_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_RETRY_CONTRACT_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-WRITE-005E 完成报告：把 operator queue item 转成 bounded retry contract substrate，展示 receipt draft、backoff policy、idempotency lock key 与 manual confirmation gates；receipt persistence 与 owner-aware review surface 的 follow-through 见 MEM-WRITE-005F，自动 retry executor 仍待下一层
  - [HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_RETRY_RECEIPT_PERSISTENCE_AND_OWNER_AWARE_OPERATOR_REVIEW_SURFACE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_RETRY_RECEIPT_PERSISTENCE_AND_OWNER_AWARE_OPERATOR_REVIEW_SURFACE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-WRITE-005F 完成报告：把 retry receipt 持久化为 `AuditLog` receipt ledger，并在 diagnostics 增加 owner-aware receipt review readout；该 surface 只承接人工确认和审查，不执行 retry、不改写 canonical facts、不扩 recommendation / commitment authority
  - [HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_RETRY_ATTEMPT_LEDGER_AND_SOURCE_REBUILD_GATE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_RETRY_ATTEMPT_LEDGER_AND_SOURCE_REBUILD_GATE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-WRITE-005G 完成报告：把 retry attempt 持久化为 `AuditLog` attempt ledger，增加 logical idempotency lock read model、duplicate lock conflict / unmatched attempt 统计与 source rebuild gate；该 gate 仍不执行 retry、不自动重建 `CreateFactInput`、不扩 recommendation / commitment authority
  - [HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_RETRY_DB_IDEMPOTENCY_SOURCE_PROOF_AND_BOUNDED_EXECUTOR_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_WRITE_RETRY_DB_IDEMPOTENCY_SOURCE_PROOF_AND_BOUNDED_EXECUTOR_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-WRITE-005H/005I/005J 完成报告：新增 `MemoryWriteRetryLock` DB guard、`MEETING_NOTE` source reconstruction proof 与 review-first bounded retry executor；executor 只在人工确认、source proof 与 DB lock 均成立时写一个 reconstructed `MemoryFact`，不重跑 meeting pipeline、不扩 commitment / recommendation authority
  - [HELM_MEMORY_PHASE_0_3_FREEZE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_PHASE_0_3_FREEZE_REPORT_V1.md)

  - [HELM_MEMORY_MYSQL_INDEX_EVIDENCE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_MYSQL_INDEX_EVIDENCE_REPORT_V1.md)

  - [HELM_MEMORY_DISTILLATION_CANDIDATE_PHASE4A_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_DISTILLATION_CANDIDATE_PHASE4A_REPORT_V1.md)

  - [HELM_MEMORY_DISTILLATION_CANDIDATE_PHASE4B_RUNTIME_PERSISTENCE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_DISTILLATION_CANDIDATE_PHASE4B_RUNTIME_PERSISTENCE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-DISTILL-006B Phase 4B 完成报告：新增 `MemoryDistillationCandidate` 持久化 substrate、review decision service 与 meeting memory pipeline 成功链路后置同步；sync/review 均保留 review-required、no canonical fact write、no auto-promotion、no recommendation ranking takeover 边界；operator UI workflow、promoted memory 与 retrieval pack promotion layer 待下一层
  - [HELM_MEMORY_DISTILLATION_CANDIDATE_PHASE4C_REVIEW_SURFACE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_MEMORY_DISTILLATION_CANDIDATE_PHASE4C_REVIEW_SURFACE_REPORT_V1.md)
    - MEM-DISTILL-006C Phase 4C 完成报告：把 `MemoryDistillationCandidate` 接入 `/memory` 第一层复核面，展示 pending queue 与 recent decisions，并提供 approve / reject / defer review action；该 action 只记录 review decision，不写 canonical `MemoryFact`、不创建 promoted memory、不改 recommendation ranking、不扩 execution authority

说明：
- 以上文件是专题细节入口，不改变“当前主干 truth”。
- 当前结构事实仍以 [project-structure.md](architecture/project-structure.md) 与 [HELM_MIGRATION_RECONCILIATION_PLAN_20260329.md](reviews/HELM_MIGRATION_RECONCILIATION_PLAN_20260329.md) 为准。
- operating-system 这层当前以 [HELM_OPERATING_SYSTEM_NEXT_STAGE_ACTIONS_REPORT.md](product/HELM_OPERATING_SYSTEM_NEXT_STAGE_ACTIONS_REPORT.md) 为准，仍然遵守 current-main reality，不等于恢复旧本地目录结构。
- onboarding / first-run / first-value 当前以 [HELM_FIRST_LOOP_PRD_V1.md](product/HELM_FIRST_LOOP_PRD_V1.md) 为 planning-only 产品入口；current-main 已经把 shared first-loop readout 接到 `/setup`、`/dashboard`、`/meetings/[id]`、`/approvals`、`/memory`、`/diagnostics`、`/reports`、`/operating`，并补了一层基于现有 `AuditLog` 的 per-user explicit return-anchor trace，以及基于 `APPROVAL_APPROVED` / `MEMORY_FACT_CONFIRMED` 的 review / write-back completion proxy readout，但这仍然只是基于现有 workspace / meeting / approval / memory truth 拼成的 read-model，不代表新的 schema、dedicated first-loop session object 或 Vertical object pack。
- 登录后首页 / dashboard 下一阶段当前以 [HELM_HOME_SURFACE_RULES_V1.md](product/HELM_HOME_SURFACE_RULES_V1.md) 为规则入口；current-main dashboard 首屏已经前置一层 `Home work entry` surface，先把 `Top 1-3 work items + Needs Your Review + Resume / Continue + light blockers` 收口到一个可直接进入动作的 work-entry block，并额外补了一层 `detail / approvals / memory` 的 `surface routing`，把 why / review / replay 更明确地下推给 dedicated work surfaces；上一轮遗留的 `detailed readouts` 旧 second-layer JSX 路径也已从首页主运行路径和源码主块中移除；同时，当用户从 Home 的 routing 卡进入 `detail / approvals / memory` 时，目标页首屏会补一层轻量 `home-surface arrival` 承接，明确“为什么送到这里、这页当前负责什么”；其中 `approvals`、`memory` 与主 `detail` 路径下的 opportunity / contact / company / meeting work surface 在 home-entry 下都已补上页面自己的 landing contract、单一主 CTA 与 second-layer disclosure，并继续压掉重复的跨页 summary；最新一层里，`approvals` 已把页头 story description、queue-side boundary context 和 queue-control 教学文案后置到 next layer，`memory` 也已把页头 story description、object-state substrate 教学文案、correction boundary、reflection history 和更重的 meeting-memory governance / replay context 后置到 next layer，richer `opportunity workspace` 里的页头 story description、`System-recommended order`、`Momentum view` 与只读 `Work Progress` context 也已继续后置到 dedicated next layer，`meeting detail` 在 home-entry 下也已把页头 story description 让位给 meeting arrival contract；dashboard 的 `detail` 卡当前也会优先把用户送进 richer opportunity workspace，避免直接掉进更薄的 detail-like 页面；但这仍只是 current-main baseline：更完整的首页状态仲裁、Top 1-3 排序强化、更细的 detail surface L1/L2 contract 和 dedicated home session object 还没有成立。
- first-loop / home surface 当前阶段冻结报告见 [HELM_FIRST_LOOP_AND_HOME_SURFACE_FREEZE_REPORT_V1.md](reviews/HELM_FIRST_LOOP_AND_HOME_SURFACE_FREEZE_REPORT_V1.md)；当前冻结结论仍然是 `已成形但仍需下一层`：shared first-loop read-model、return-anchor trace、per-user adoption readout、dashboard 首屏 work-entry surface 和 targeted continuity e2e hardening 已成立，但这仍然不是 dedicated first-loop lifecycle system，也不是完整首页 IA 重写。
- 组织 operating truth 当前以 [HELM_OPERATING_CONSTITUTION_V1.md](product/HELM_OPERATING_CONSTITUTION_V1.md)、[HELM_ROLE_AUDIENCE_FOUNDATION_V1.md](product/HELM_ROLE_AUDIENCE_FOUNDATION_V1.md)、[HELM_ORGANIZATIONAL_MEMORY_FOUNDATION_V1.md](product/HELM_ORGANIZATIONAL_MEMORY_FOUNDATION_V1.md)、[HELM_GOAL_CAMPAIGN_FOUNDATION_V1.md](product/HELM_GOAL_CAMPAIGN_FOUNDATION_V1.md) 及其 baseline freeze 包为准，当前仍只是第一轮 foundation，不是完整 operating platform。

## 保留专题索引

以下入口保留为**历史专题 / baseline freeze / alignment / acceptance** 索引。
它们用于保持报告、验收和 delivery 资产可发现，不改变“当前主干 reality”。

### Shared Agent / Pilot

- [SHARED_AGENT_PRIMITIVES_BASELINE_V1.md](product/SHARED_AGENT_PRIMITIVES_BASELINE_V1.md)
- [SHARED_AGENT_SEMANTICS_ACCEPTANCE_REPORT.md](reviews/SHARED_AGENT_SEMANTICS_ACCEPTANCE_REPORT.md)
- [SHARED_AGENT_OPERATIONAL_SURFACE_BASELINE_V1.md](product/SHARED_AGENT_OPERATIONAL_SURFACE_BASELINE_V1.md)
- [SHARED_AGENT_OPERATIONAL_SURFACE_ACCEPTANCE_REPORT.md](reviews/SHARED_AGENT_OPERATIONAL_SURFACE_ACCEPTANCE_REPORT.md)
- [SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_READINESS_V1.md](pilot/SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_READINESS_V1.md)
- [SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_RUNBOOK_V1.md](pilot/SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_RUNBOOK_V1.md)
- [SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_OBSERVATION_TEMPLATE_V1.md](pilot/SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_OBSERVATION_TEMPLATE_V1.md)
- [SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_READINESS_REPORT.md](reviews/SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_READINESS_REPORT.md)
- [SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_SESSION_REPORT_TEMPLATE.md](reviews/SHARED_AGENT_PILOT_SESSION_REPORT_TEMPLATE.md)
- [shared-agent-outcome-snapshot.ts](../scripts/shared-agent-outcome-snapshot.ts)
- customer success 仍是 richest proving ground，review-request detail 是 first thin adjacent adoption，success-check detail 是 second thin adjacent adoption，expansion-review detail 是 third thin adjacent adoption
- shared operational queue/card layer 目前只在 customer success queue/cards 上得到证明
- shared agent pilot readiness 现在只回答“当前 surface 是否足够支持人工 pilot 评估”和“现有 signal 到底能测什么”

  - Helm 战略左右互博综合推演：基于内部产品 / 架构反方、外部市场 / GTM 反方、repo truth 与公开市场信号，收口未来 90 天产品、市场、销售、GTM、渠道与目标情景；明确 12 个月不追市场占有率，优先追 2 个 proof、3-5 个 paid pilots、0 boundary incident、可复制 Pack A SOP、定价口径清晰和 founder-led sales / delivery 分离
- [HELM_COMMERCIAL_PROMOTION_PACK_WORKER_SKILL_PLAN.md](product/HELM_COMMERCIAL_PROMOTION_PACK_WORKER_SKILL_PLAN.md)
  - Internal Commercial Promotion Pack 规划：把 founder-led GTM 拆成 6 个 review-first artifact worker，并新增 `evals/commercial-promotion/worker-artifact-cases.json` + `npm run eval:commercial-promotion` 作为 Phase 1 offline quality gate；A 市场进一步新增 `evals/pack-a/pilot-readiness-cases.json` + `npm run eval:pack-a-pilot-readiness`，把候选评分、scope call、Week 0 合同/DPA/数据/角色 gate 和 4 个 Pack A Skill 集成覆盖打通；支撑 20 个候选 alias、8-10 通验证电话、Top 2-3 scope call、1 个 paid pilot ready 与 0 boundary incident；不做自动触达、自动发送、自动报价、自动 CRM 写回、自动发布或 Phase 3 runtime overclaim
- [packs/PACK_A_DESIGN_PARTNER_EVALUATION_V1.md](sales/packs/PACK_A_DESIGN_PARTNER_EVALUATION_V1.md)
  - Pack A 第一个 design partner 候选评估表：100 分制辅助创始人筛选，不锁死最终决策
- [packs/PACK_A_OPC_MARKET_VALIDATION_SYSTEM.md](sales/packs/PACK_A_OPC_MARKET_VALIDATION_SYSTEM.md)
  - Pack A OPC 市场验证系统：用失败事件、owner、数据、proof、付费和边界六项评分，驱动 30 天 design partner 验证节奏；左右互博后补充 review-first 销售表达修正、¥30k/¥50k/¥80k 价格测试、Phase 3 calibration 边界、分层验收门和 GTM / implementation 最小责任分工；当前可用 `npm run eval:pack-a-pilot-readiness` 做 alias-only readiness gate
- [packs/PACK_A_OPC_WEEK1_EXECUTION_PACK.md](sales/packs/PACK_A_OPC_WEEK1_EXECUTION_PACK.md)
  - Pack A OPC Week 1 执行包：用 20 个候选 alias、公开安全字段、每日节奏和交接门绕开等待私域名单的阻塞
- [packs/PACK_A_OPC_CANDIDATE_TRACKER_TEMPLATE.csv](sales/packs/PACK_A_OPC_CANDIDATE_TRACKER_TEMPLATE.csv)
  - Pack A OPC 候选 tracker 模板：可导入飞书 / Excel，只存 alias 与评分字段，不提交真实客户名单
- [packs/PACK_A_DESIGN_PARTNER_INTERVIEW_PROTOCOL.md](sales/packs/PACK_A_DESIGN_PARTNER_INTERVIEW_PROTOCOL.md)

## 关于旧本地 Helm 迁移

旧本地 `helm/` 子目录里的 12 个提交只作为**迁移意图 archive** 使用：

- 不做机械 replay
- 不做 mass rebase
- 不把旧 `apps/helm-app` / `packages/helm-control` 目录当成当前主干 truth

真正的当前主干迁移策略，请以：

- [HELM_MIGRATION_RECONCILIATION_PLAN_20260329.md](reviews/HELM_MIGRATION_RECONCILIATION_PLAN_20260329.md)

为准。
